huṃphaṭkārayutena tu 
huṃphaṭkāravidarbhiṇaḥ 
huṃphaṭkāravidarbhitam 
huṃ vaṣaṭ phaṭ krameṇa tu 
hūyate tadvidaiḥ sadā 
hṛccakre tu samākhyātāḥ 
hṛcchiraśca śikhā varma 
hṛcchiraśca śikhā varma 
hṛcchiraśca śikhāṃ tathā 
hṛtkaṇṭhatālubhrūmadhya- 
hṛtkaṇṭhatālumadhyagam 
hṛtpadmasaṃdhimadhye tu 
hṛtpadmaṃ tu yadā prāptaḥ 
hṛtpadmaṃ darśayedyā tu 
hṛtpadmaṃ yāvadāgataḥ 
hṛtpadmaṃ ṣoḍaśacchadam 
hṛtpadmātsarvato vrajet 
hṛtpadmādūrdhvaparyantaṃ 
hṛtpadmādyāvadayanaṃ 
hṛtpadmādyāvaśaktitaḥ 
hṛtpadmādyāva śaktitaḥ 
hṛtpadmādyāva śaktyūrdhvaṃ 
hṛtpadmāntaṃ tu vai haṃsaś 
hṛtpadme viniveśayet 
hṛtvā tvaṣṭaśataṃ devi 
hṛtsthaṃ chittvāstrakhaḍgena 
hṛtsthaṃ tatsaṃsmaretpriye 
hṛdantaṃ kalpayedyāvat 
hṛdabjaṃ yāvadāgataḥ 
hṛdayaṃ guhyamityuktaṃ 
hṛdayaṃ madhyadeśe tu 
hṛdayaṃ yasya roditi 
hṛdayaṃ raktavarṇābhaṃ 
hṛdayaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ caiva 
hṛdayaṃ śuṣyate yasya 
hṛdayāttu vinirgataḥ 
hṛdayātsaṃpravartate 
hṛdayādīṃstataḥ pañca 
hṛdayādudayasthānāt 
hṛdaye nābhideśe ca 
hṛdayenaiva pūjayet 
hṛdayordhve tu kaṇṭhādho 
hṛdā trirāhutiṃ dattvā 
hṛdādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ 
hṛdādau daśakaṃ hutiḥ 
hṛdādyāni yathākramam 
hṛdādyāvaraṇasthānāṃ 
hṛdādyā vācakāstāsāṃ 
hṛdādyaiḥ pañcabhiścāṅgair 
hṛdā vai jalabinduṃ tu 
hṛdā saṃkalpya vāgīśīṃ 
hṛdi grīvāṃsapṛṣṭhe tu 
hṛdi citsaṃhṛtā bhavet 
hṛdi tyāgo bhavettasya 
hṛdgataḥ punaruttiṣṭhed 
hṛdgude nābhikaṇṭhe ca 
heti śiṣyasya śirasi 
hetukartā maheśānaḥ 
hetudṛṣṭāntavādibhiḥ 
hetuniṣṭhāni vākyāni 
hetuvādavivarjitam 
hetuśāstraparā ye tu 
hetuśāstraṃ ca yalloke 
hemakūṭasya yāmyena 
hemakūṭasya saumyena 
hemakūṭo mahātejās 
hemacīnāmbaradharo 
hemacīnāmbaraḥ śubhaḥ 
hematvaṃ pratipadyate 
hemapaṭṭaparīdhānā 
hemapatraiḥ sugandhibhiḥ 
hemaprākāraracitaṃ 
hemaprākāraśikharaiś 
hemavarṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
hemaśyāmāśca yoṣitaḥ 
hemasaṃjñā vasūnāṃ tu 
hemāṇḍaṃ tu purāsṛṣṭaṃ 
hemābhaṃ prākcatuṣkaṃ tad 
hemābhā pītavasanā 
hemābhāḥ śaṅkarāḥ proktāḥ 
heyādhvānamadhaḥ kurvan 
heyopādeyataḥ sthitāḥ 
heyopādeyapāśānāṃ 
helādaṇḍāhatāyāśca 
haimī citrarathasya tu 
hairaṇyamatulaṃ prāptā 
hotavyāni na saṃśayaḥ 
hotavyāni varānane 
hotavyā niṣkṛtirbhinnā 
hotā jāgara eva ca 
homayedyastu sādhakaḥ 
homayennaramāṃsasya 
homayennāmasammiśraṃ 
homaṃ kṛtvā varānane 
homaṃ kṛtvā visarjayet 
homaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
homāttacca tritattvakam 
homātsiddhiḥ parā bhavet 
homitaṃ siddhijananaṃ 
homena ca japena ca 
homenaiva tu saṃśodhya 
homaireva tribhistribhiḥ 
hrasetsaṃkrāntirekaikā 
hrasvakoṭisamanvitau 
hrasvadīrghaprayogataḥ 
hrasvadīrghaplutānvitam 
hrasvadīrghavibhāgena 
hrasvadīrghavibhāgena 
hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutaṃ param 
hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutaṃ sūkṣmam 
hrasvaḥ putravināśanaḥ 
hlādayantīva gātrāṇi
